## Decomposition Artifact

This artifact decomposes `Test-Flight-Improv/Group-Chat-Feature/Private_group_chat_reliability_test_matrix_COMPLETE_1.md` row-by-row for downstream rollout execution. The decomposition preserves every source row ID as the session ID because all row IDs are filename-safe. No rows were merged by section, seam, gate family, or likely implementation file.

Correction status: `PREREQ-GM-MULTI-PARTY-DEVICE-HARNESS` is a shared, accepted/closed prerequisite for GM rows requiring exact multi-party Flutter device proof. It is not a source matrix row and does not close source rows by itself. GM-001 through GM-007 are now closed by their own row-specific artifacts; GM-008 and later unresolved rows remain open.

Rows with existing adjacent tests are still kept as row-owned sessions unless a downstream plan proves exact current coverage for that exact source row. The source matrix marks the rows Open, and several adjacent tests cover only part of the user-visible contract.

## Overall Closure Bar

The rollout is not closed until every source row has a final row-level truth update with concrete evidence. For each row-owned session, closure requires one of: exact passing code/test evidence and source matrix status update to `Closed` or `Covered`; explicit repo-external proof with captured artifact references; or an explicit unsupported-product-scope note backed by current product contract evidence.

A broad group-chat reliability pass is not enough. Later closure work must report final truth per source row, including optional, repo-external, duplicate, already-covered, or unsupported rows. No such rows were omitted in this decomposition.

- Final verdict policy: use exactly one of `closed`, `accepted_with_explicit_follow_up`, `residual_only`, or `still_open`; use `closed` only when every row required by this breakdown is resolved with row-specific evidence.

## Row Traceability Rule

Every source row maps to exactly one session ID or one explicit `duplicate_of` relationship. This matrix has no duplicate source IDs and no `duplicate_of` relationships, so every row maps one-to-one to its preserved source row ID. Later closure work must report final truth per source row, not only per broad subsystem or test family.

## Evidence Map

Evidence keys are used in the row session tables to keep the file readable. Each key names concrete likely code-entry files, adjacent tests, named gates, and proof ownership. Row plans must narrow these candidates to exact row-owned tests before marking a row covered.

## Dependency Pass

Rows do not depend on one another by default. This correction adds one explicit shared prerequisite session for GM rows whose required closure proof needs multi-party Flutter app devices: `PREREQ-GM-MULTI-PARTY-DEVICE-HARNESS`.

The multi-party Flutter device harness now exists as accepted repo-owned prerequisite support, not terminal external-fixture scope. GM-001 consumed that prerequisite and is now `Covered` by its own row-specific A/B/C relay proof; GM-002 also consumed it and is now `Covered` by its own row-specific A/B/C/D relay proof; GM-003 consumed it and is now `Covered` by its own row-specific offline-add A/B/C/D relay proof; GM-004 consumed it and is now `Covered` by its own row-specific remove-online A/B/C relay proof; GM-005 consumed it and is now `Covered` by its own row-specific stale-offline removal A/B/C relay proof; GM-006 consumed it and is now `Covered` by its own row-specific immediate remove/re-add A/B/C relay proof. The prerequisite-shaped device artifacts remain useful but non-closing for source rows. Other rows that mention fake network, 3-party E2E, relay failover, raw envelope tampering, race detector, or long-soak proof surfaces still own their own row evidence unless they explicitly reuse this prerequisite.

Existing two-simulator, two-device-plus-CLI, relay-nightly, and invite-status display fixtures remain useful references, but they are not sufficient closure proof for GM-001 through GM-007 by themselves. The accepted prerequisite harness removes the missing-harness blocker only; GM-001 through GM-007 are `Covered` only because their own row-specific artifacts passed.

## Shared Prerequisite Sessions

| Session ID | Row disposition | Classification | Scope | Owner files and reusable references | Required harness behavior |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PREREQ-GM-MULTI-PARTY-DEVICE-HARNESS | needs_code_and_tests | accepted/closed prerequisite | Reusable Flutter integration/device harness support now exists for row-specific private-group reliability proofs. GM-001-shaped A/B/C proof and GM-002-shaped A/B/C/D proof passed as prerequisite validation only; GM-003 later added row-owned offline-add scenario support and closed by its own artifact; GM-004 later added row-owned remove-online proof support and closed by its own artifact; GM-005 later added row-owned stale-offline removal proof support and closed by its own artifact; GM-006 later added row-owned immediate remove/re-add proof support and closed by its own artifact; GM-007 later added row-owned history-boundary proof support and closed by its own artifact. GM-008 and later GM rows should reuse this harness rather than invent row-local orchestration. | Owners: `integration_test/scripts/run_group_multi_party_device_real.dart`, `integration_test/group_multi_party_device_real_harness.dart`, `integration_test/scripts/group_multi_party_device_criteria.dart`, `test/integration/group_multi_party_device_criteria_test.dart`. Gate docs classify the host criteria test and manual orchestrator without promoting them into frozen named gates. | Accepted evidence: criteria helper test passed with 11 tests; targeted analyzer passed; `./scripts/run_test_gates.sh groups` passed; `./scripts/run_test_gates.sh completeness-check` passed with `731/731` files classified; `git diff --check` passed; GM-001-shaped artifact `gmp_1778401870395_gm001_orchestrator_verdict.json` is `ok: true`; GM-002-shaped artifact `gmp_1778402193277_gm002_orchestrator_verdict.json` is `ok: true`. These artifacts prove the harness, not GM source-row closure; later row-specific GM-001 through GM-007 artifacts close those rows. |

## Row Checkpoint Commit Policy

- After each session closure is durably written and verified, the controller should create a local checkpoint commit for that session before starting the next session.
- This is a rollout-specific policy for this breakdown, not a generic skill requirement.
- Before staging, run `git status --short` and inspect scoped diffs for the just-completed session.
- Stage explicit paths only. Never use `git add .`.
- Commit only files owned by the just-completed session: its plan file, row-owned code/test files, and closure docs updated for that session.
- Do not stage unrelated dirty files, user edits, generated artifacts, or files being edited by another active session.
- Do not commit while another session is actively editing the same breakdown, matrix, inventory, or test files.
- Blocked or `still_open` rows may still get checkpoint commits, but only after the blocker is durably recorded in the source matrix/breakdown and the commit message clearly says it is a blocker checkpoint.
- If the worktree contains unrelated dirty changes, leave them unstaged and mention them in the session report.
- If a clean scoped commit cannot be made safely, record `checkpoint_skipped` in the session notes with the reason, then continue only if the dirty state is safe for the next session.

Recommended commit message format:

- Accepted/covered row: `<ROW-ID>: close <short row summary>`
- Blocked row: `<ROW-ID>: record <short row summary> blocker`
- Prerequisite/harness row: `<ROW-ID>: add <short prerequisite summary>`

## Ordered Session Breakdown

Default order is explicit prerequisites, then P0 rows in source order, then P1 rows in source order, then P2 rows in source order. This artifact has one explicit GM prerequisite session and no final closure-only session. The prerequisite is inserted before GM-001 without renumbering historical source-row order values.

## Downstream Execution Path

Use this artifact as the input to the implementation-session pipeline. For each row in `## Session Ledger` order:

1. Create or refresh the intended row plan path: `<source-stem>-session-<session-id>-plan.md`.
2. `PREREQ-GM-MULTI-PARTY-DEVICE-HARNESS` is already accepted; GM-001, GM-002, and GM-003 have consumed it and are now covered by row-specific proof. Every other row plan stays scoped to the single source row unless the row itself proves a local prerequisite is required.
3. Execute the plan, run the named gates, and capture exact evidence.
4. Update the source matrix row and this breakdown or adjacent closure notes with the final row truth.
5. After Session Closure and ledger updates are durably written and verified, apply `## Row Checkpoint Commit Policy` before selecting the next runnable session.
6. Do not mark a broad subsystem as closed unless every source row mapped to that subsystem has row-specific evidence.

Recommended next controller: `$implementation-session-pipeline-orchestrator` against this breakdown artifact.
